   <script type="text/javascript">
    function fetchMoreLatestEvents(modid, direction)
 {        
         jQuery.ajax({
                     type : 'POST',
                     dataType : 'json',
                     url : "http://www.socawarriors.net/index.php?option=com_jevents&ttoption=com_jevents&typeaheadtask=gwejson&file=fetchlatestevents&path=module&folder=mod_jevents_latest&token=1c90d676dbe477cd93ac730ad215b8a6",
                     data : {'json':JSON.stringify({'modid':modid, 'direction':direction})},
                     contentType: "application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=utf-8",
                     scriptCharset: "utf-8"
             })                        
                 .done(function( data ){                    
                     jQuery("#mod_events_latest_"+modid+"_data").replaceWith(data.html);
                     try {
                         document.getElementById("mod_events_latest_"+modid+"_data").parentNode.scrollIntoView({block: "start", behavior: "smooth"});
                     }
                     catch (e) {
                     }
                 })
                 .fail(function(x) {
         alert('fail '+x);
                 });
 }
 (function()
 				{
 					if(typeof jQuery == 'undefined')
 						return;
 					
 					jQuery(function($)
 					{
 						if($.fn.squeezeBox)
 						{
 							$( 'a.modal' ).squeezeBox({ parse: 'rel' });
 				
 							$( 'img.modal' ).each( function( i, el )
 							{
 								$(el).squeezeBox({
 									handler: 'image',
 									url: $( el ).attr( 'src' )
 								});
 							})
 						}
 						else if(typeof(SqueezeBox) !== 'undefined')
 						{
 							$( 'img.modal' ).each( function( i, el )
 							{
 								SqueezeBox.assign( el, 
 								{
 									handler: 'image',
 									url: $( el ).attr( 'src' )
 								});
 							});
 						}
 						
 						function jModalClose() 
 						{
 							if(typeof(SqueezeBox) == 'object')
 								SqueezeBox.close();
 							else
 								ARK.squeezeBox.close();
 						}
 					
 					});
 				})();
   </script>

         <h4>

            <div class="magazine-item-main">
             <div class="article-title">
              <h3 itemprop="name">
               <a href="/mens-u15/20894-ttfa-nlcb-elite-u-15-boys-show-progress-on-the-training-pitch.html" itemprop="url">
                TTFA/NLCB Elite U-15 Boys show progress on the training pitch
               </a>
              </h3>
             </div>
             <aside class="article-aside clearfix">
              <dl class="article-info muted">
               <dt class="article-info-term">
                Details
               </dt>
               <dd class="hidden">

             <div class="magazine-item-ct">
              <p>
               While the World Cup is in full swing in Russia, several of this country’s aspiring international footballers are facing the grind four days a week as the TTFA/NLCB Elite U-15 Boys programme continues at a brisk pace at the TTFA Home of Football, Ato Boldon Stadium.
              </p>
             </div>

           </div>
           <div class="item ">
            <div class="magazine-item-media">
             <span class="media-mask">
             </span>
             <div class="pull-left item-image">
              <img alt="Mitchell signs with Albanian Superliga club Kastrioti." class="caption" itemprop="thumbnailUrl" src="/images/Jabari-Mitchell-vs-Guadeloupe.jpg" title="Mitchell signs with Albanian Superliga club Kastrioti."/>
             </div>

            <div class="magazine-item-main">
             <div class="article-title">
              <h3 itemprop="name">
               <a href="/foreign-based/20891-mitchell-signs-with-albanian-superliga-club-ks-kastrioti.html" itemprop="url">
                Mitchell signs with Albanian Superliga club KS Kastrioti
               </a>
              </h3>
             </div>

             <div class="magazine-item-ct">
              <p>
               Former Trinidad and Tobago Under 20 Men’s captain Jabari Mitchell has signed a one-year deal with Albanian Superliga club KS Kastrioti.
              </p>

            <div class="magazine-item-media">

Crane)" class="caption" itemprop="thumbnailUrl" src="/images/Connection-Marcus-Joseph-vs-Stars-June-2018.jpg" title="Photo: W Connection ace Marcus Joseph controls the ball ahead of North East Stars captain and defender Sean Bateau during the Savonetta Boys 2-0 group stage win in the 2018 First Citizens Cup at the Ato Boldon Stadium on Jun. 16, 2018.                </span>

            <div class="magazine-item-main">
             <div class="article-title">
              <h3 itemprop="name">
               <a href="/league-cup/20888-marcus-joseph-seals-another-connection-win-with-sublime-chip-while-civic-rebounds.html" itemprop="url">
                Marcus Joseph seals another Connection win with sublime chip while Civic rebounds
               </a>
              </h3>
             </div>
             <aside class="article-aside clearfix">
              <dl class="article-info muted">
               <dt class="article-info-term">
                Details
               </dt>
               <dd class="hidden">
               </dd>

             <div class="magazine-item-ct">
              <p>
               W Connection took command of Abercrombie Group in the 2018 First Citizens Cup on Saturday evening with six points but had to settle for a 2-0 Match Day Two win over North East Stars, a side the Savonetta Boys had humiliated 7-1 a fortnight ago in the season-opening Charity Shield.
              </p>

           <div class="item ">
            <div class="magazine-item-media">
             <span class="media-mask">
             </span>
             <div class="pull-left item-image">
              <img alt="DJW reveals limited Home of Football info, admits to breaking up contracts to avoid tender." class="caption" itemprop="thumbnailUrl" src="/images/DJW-Infantino.jpg" title="DJW reveals limited Home of Football info, admits to breaking up contracts to avoid tender."/>
             </div>
             <span class="category-name cat-red" title="Category: ">
              <a href="/federation-news.html">
               <span itemprop="genre">

            <div class="magazine-item-main">
             <div class="article-title">
              <h3 itemprop="name">
               <a href="/federation-news/20887-djw-reveals-limited-home-of-football-info-admits-to-breaking-up-contracts-to-avoid-tender.html" itemprop="url">
                DJW reveals limited Home of Football info, admits to breaking up contracts to avoid tender
               </a>
              </h3>
             </div>
             <aside class="article-aside clearfix">
              <dl class="article-info muted">
               <dt class="article-info-term">
                Details
               </dt>
               <dd class="hidden">
               </dd>
               <dd class="createdby hasTooltip" itemprop="author" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" title="Written by ">
                <span itemprop="name">
                 Lasana Liburd (Wired868)
                </span>
               </dd>
               <dd class="create">
                <i class="fa fa-calendar">
                </i>
                <time datetime="2018-06-13T03:48:37-04:00" itemprop="dateCreated">
                 Created: 13 June 2018
                </time>
               </dd>
               <dd class="hits">
                <i class="fa fa-eye">
                </i>
                <meta content="UserPageVisits:227" itemprop="interactionCount"/>
                Hits: 227
               </dd>
              </dl>
             </aside>
             <div class="magazine-item-ct">
              <p>
               Trinidad and Tobago Football Association (TTFA) president David John-Williams split FIFA funding for the Home of Football project between 15 companies—according to information he sent to Board members—in a move that allowed the administrator to avoid putting contracts up for tender.
              </p>
             </div>

            <div class="magazine-item-ct">
             <p>
              Trinidad and Tobago Football Association (TTFA) president David John-Williams split FIFA funding for the Home of Football project between 15 companies—according to information he sent to Board members—in a move that allowed the administrator to avoid putting contracts up for tender.

               John-Williams praised and censured at EGM
              </a>
             </h3>

            <aside class="article-aside clearfix">

            <div class="magazine-item-ct">
             <p>
              President of the T&amp;T Football Association David John-Williams came in for praises for his genuine efforts to construct the now famous Home of Football in Balmain, Couva, but at the end of Wednesday’s reconvened Extraordinary General Meeting (EGM) held at the nearby National Cycling Centre (NCC), a motion was moved to censure him for his approach.
             </p>

             <h3 itemprop="name">
              <a href="/federation-news/20885-ttfa-2016-financial-statement-approved.html" itemprop="url">
               TTFA 2016 financial statement approved
              </a>
             </h3>

            <div class="magazine-item-ct">
             <p>
              <strong>
               Questions linger about Home of Football but…
              </strong>
              <br/>
              <br/>
              PRESIDENT OF the Trinidad and Tobago Football Association (TTFA) David John-Williams says he has local football’s best interest at heart, following the passing of the 2016 financial statements at a five-hour long Extraordinary General Meeting (EGM) on Wednesday at the National Cycling Centre, Couva.
             </p>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="col col-xs-12 col-sm-4 magazine-item">
           <div class="magazine-item-media">
            <span class="media-mask">
            </span>
            <div class="pull-left item-image">
             <img alt="TTFA worried over automatic spots." class="caption" itemprop="thumbnailUrl" src="/images/2026-World-Cup.png" title="TTFA worried over automatic spots."/>
            </div>
            <span class="category-name cat-red" title="Category: ">
             <a href="/federation-news.html">
              <span itemprop="genre">
               Federation
              </span>
             </a>
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="magazine-item-main">
            <div class="article-title">
             <h3 itemprop="name">
              <a href="/federation-news/20884-ttfa-worried-over-automatic-spots-fifa-world-cup-returns-to-the-region.html" itemprop="url">
               TTFA worried over automatic spots, FIFA World Cup returns to the Region
              </a>
             </h3>
            </div>
            <aside class="article-aside clearfix">
             <dl class="article-info muted">
              <dt class="article-info-term">
               Details
              </dt>
              <dd class="hidden">
              </dd>
              <dd class="createdby hasTooltip" itemprop="author" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" title="Written by ">
               <span itemprop="name">
                Jelani Beckles (T&amp;T Newsday)
               </span>
              </dd>
              <dd class="published hasTooltip" title="Published: ">
               <i class="icon-calendar">
               </i>
               <time datetime="2018-06-14T03:48:48-04:00" itemprop="datePublished">
                14 June 2018
               </time>
              </dd>
              <dd class="create">
               <i class="fa fa-calendar">
               </i>
               <time datetime="2018-06-14T03:48:48-04:00" itemprop="dateCreated">
                Created: 14 June 2018
               </time>
              </dd>
              <dd class="hits">
               <i class="fa fa-eye">
               </i>
               <meta content="UserPageVisits:641" itemprop="interactionCount"/>
               Hits: 641
              </dd>
             </dl>
            </aside>
            <div class="magazine-item-ct">
             <p>
              <strong>
               US, Mexico, Canada to host 2026 World Cup but…
              </strong>
              <br/>
              <br/>
              TT Football Association president David John-Williams is happy but not ready to dance following the news that the 2026 World Cup will be played in CONCACAF. At the FIFA Congress yesterday, it was announced that the joint bid by USA, Canada and Mexico won the rights for the 2026 showpiece, where 48 teams will feature for the first time. The CONCACAF region has been awarded six and a half spots. It has not been determined whether all three host countries will get automatic berths.
             </p>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>

             <p>
              It was a good week to be a BOCA Knight. Over the last week, BOCA cemented themselves as the top team in the Western Conference if not the league. Then, in a cross-conference match, they treated Northshore United likewise with a decisive 4-1 win.

             <p>
              The Confederation of North, Central America and Caribbean Association Football (Concacaf) has announced the details for the 2018 Concacaf Girls’ Under-15 Championship. This year’s girls’ under-15, which will be the largest Concacaf tournament ever for female participants, will feature the participation of a record amount of Concacaf Member Associations and two invited teams from UEFA.

            <div class="magazine-item-ct">
             <p>
              I had planned my column this week to revisit some of the top European football leagues, and of course the Champions League final where the most entertaining club in Europe – Liverpool – was unlucky to lose to Real Madrid; Salah’s injury was a massive game changer. Those of you who know me are well aware that I have been a lifelong Liverpool fan since the days when Roger Hunt was bulging the old onion bag with goal after goal. But we will save the top European leagues for another time and I will preview the upcoming 2018-2019 season after the World Cup.
             </p>

          <div class="magazine-category-title ">
           <h2>
            <a href="/beach-soccer.html" title="Beach Soccer">
             Beach Soccer
            </a>
           </h2>
          </div>
          <div class="magazine-item magazine-leading">
           <div class="magazine-item-media">
            <span class="media-mask">
            </span>
            <span class="category-name " title="Category: ">
             <a href="/beach-soccer.html">
              <span itemprop="genre">
               Beach Soccer
              </span>
             </a>
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="magazine-item-main">
            <div class="article-title">
             <h3 itemprop="name">
              <a href="/beach-soccer/20413-black-rock-is-beach-soccer-turf.html" itemprop="url">
               Black Rock is beach soccer turf
              </a>
             </h3>
            </div>
            <aside class="article-aside clearfix">
             <dl class="article-info muted">
              <dt class="article-info-term">
               Details
              </dt>
              <dd class="hidden">
              </dd>
              <dd class="published hasTooltip" title="Published: ">
               <i class="icon-calendar">
               </i>
               <time datetime="2017-11-30T06:31:57-04:00" itemprop="datePublished">
                30 November 2017
               </time>
              </dd>
              <dd class="create">
               <i class="fa fa-calendar">
               </i>
               <time datetime="2017-11-30T06:31:57-04:00" itemprop="dateCreated">
                Created: 30 November 2017
               </time>
              </dd>
             </dl>
            </aside>
            <div class="magazine-item-ct">
             <p>
              Eight years ago, the Tobago Beach Soccer Championship was first hosted and at the time, was the first formal introduction of the fastest growing version of football to T&amp;T.
             </p>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="magazine-item link-item">
           <div class="col col-media">
            <div class="pull-left item-image">
             <img alt="" class="caption" itemprop="thumbnailUrl" src="/images/stories/shoreline_beach_soccer_club_tobago_2017_champions.jpg" title="Shoreline Beach Soccer Club was the champion women’s team at the 8th Annual Tobago Beach Soccer Championships in Black Rock Tobago November 10-12. Shoreline defeated fellow USA-based team NorCal 7-4 in the final."/>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="col col-content">
            <aside class="article-aside">

               </time>
              </dd>
              <dd class="create">
               <i class="fa fa-calendar">
               </i>

              </dd>
             </dl>
            </aside>
            <div class="article-title">
             <h3 itemprop="name">
              <a href="/beach-soccer/20330-shoreline-aq-lions-cop-tobago-beach-soccer-titles.html" itemprop="url">
               Shoreline, AQ Lions cop Tobago Beach Soccer titles
              </a>
             </h3>
            </div>
